      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL0)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL1)
      linkParticle: s32'ven_charaball_burst'
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
      ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 1
      ignoreFinishStop: 1
    endUpon: 
    upon: (SIGNAL1)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL0)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL1)
      linkParticle: s32'ven_charaball_end'
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
      ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 1
      ignoreFinishStop: 1
    endUpon: 
    upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
        if: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
          displayModel: 0
          createObject: s32'VEN_charaball_flash', (PLAYER)
          sendSignalToAction: s32'VEN502_EnemyBall_detail', (SIGNAL0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
          displayModel: 1
          createObject: s32'VEN_charaball_flash', (PLAYER)
          sendSignalToAction: s32'VEN502_EnemyBall_detail', (SIGNAL1)
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
  endLabel: 
  exitState: 
  beginLabel: s32'end'
  sprite: s32'null', 30
endState:
